Wang Jinyu Directs Troops to Suppress Bandits in Pingxiang 70

Armies on the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Border Unite as One

Chiang Orders the 18th Division to Replenish and Restore to Original State

Han and Xu Divisions Ordered to Enter Jiangxi to Suppress Bandits

Nanchang Communication: The Xiushui, Wuning, Tonggu, Wanzai, Lianhua, Pingjiang, Liuyang, Tongshan, and Tongcheng areas on the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi border have been severely devastated by the bandits led by Kong Hechong, Li Shi, and Li Can. Since the Fourth Route Army conquered Pingjiang and Liuyang, Kong and Li bandits have been wreaking havoc on Xiushui and Tonggu and threatening Wuning and Ruichang. Therefore, Commander-in-Chief Chiang appointed Wang Jinyu as the bandit suppression director of the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi border, responsible for clearing the bandits in that area. According to a telegram from Pingxiang, Wang Jinyu arrived in Pingxiang from Hunan on the 12th and immediately led his troops to suppress the bandits in Lianhua and Wanzai. As for Hao Mengling's 54th Division under Wang's command, after entering Jiangxi from Hubei, it advanced from Nanxun to aid Wuning. Yesterday, Staff Officer Wu of the division's office in the province received a telegram from Division Commander Hao, stating that his troops had arrived at the designated location and that he would lead the division headquarters to Wuning on the Eastern Day. He has established contact with the divisions of Chen Guangzhong, Tao Guang, and Xie Bin in Xiushui and Tonggu and has united with Wang Jinyu's troops stationed in Pingxiang. The various units have begun searching and suppressing the bandits in the Wugong Mountains area bordering the three provinces and have set a deadline for clearing them out.

On the first day of this month, the 18th Division of the Ninth Route Army fought fiercely with bandits at Longgangxu. Due to the dangerous terrain, the 52nd and 53rd Brigades were completely wiped out, losing four to five thousand rifles. Division Commander Zhang and Brigade Commander Wang were captured by the communists. It is rumored that Zhang and Wang died unyielding, but it is not known for sure. It is said that Commander-in-Chief Chiang greatly appreciated and regretted Division Commander Zhang's brave bandit suppression, which resulted in heavy sacrifices. He has approved the division's replenishment and restoration to its original state to show encouragement. However, as of now, the whereabouts of Division Commander Zhang are still unknown. Commander-in-Chief Lu and all walks of life are deeply saddened. Mrs. Zhang has also gone to Wuhan to find ways to rescue him. In addition, Vice Division Commander Dai was recently appointed as the Nanchang Garrison Commander and took office on the 10th, gathering officers and soldiers to give a speech, urging them to pay attention to winter defense and consolidate security amid the tense bandit suppression. Dai has been in the 18th Division for a long time, and there is talk of him acting as the division commander of the 18th Division. According to military sources, after receiving the news of the defeat of the Jiangxi bandit suppression army, Chiang ordered Han Deqin's 52nd Division and Xu Tingyao's 4th Division to enter Jiangxi to assist in the suppression. Recently, Lu received a telegram from Division Commander Han, stating that the 154th and 156th Brigades under Xu Zhibai of his unit could be concentrated in Nanchang before the 15th. Xu's 4th Division is also being transported from Beijing to Jiangxi and will arrive within a week. (January 14)

Anhui Province Increases Salt Tax Surcharge in Northern Anhui 71

Chambers of Commerce Unanimously Oppose

Bengbu Communication: The salt tax surcharge in Anhui Province was originally collected in the counties along the Anhui coast. Recently, the provincial government, due to financial difficulties with the provincial defense military, decided to extend the collection to Zhejiang salt in southern Anhui and Huai and Lu salt in northern Anhui, uniformly increasing the provincial defense surcharge by two yuan and forty cents per load, following the precedent of the Anhui coast. Special bureaus were established in Tunxi in southern Anhui and Bengbu in northern Anhui to collect the surcharge, and Duan Shizhang was appointed as the director of the Anhui Provincial Defense Salt Tax Surcharge Northern Anhui Collection Bureau. After being appointed, Duan came to Bengbu at the end of last month and established the bureau in the residence of a Mr. Xi on Zhongxin Street, scheduled to start collecting on the 10th. The chambers of commerce in various counties and towns in northern Anhui believe that the Anhui provincial salt surcharge was previously canceled by the Anhui Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation's telegram to the provincial government, and it was not approved. They now believe that the burden is too heavy and strongly oppose it, sending representatives Yang Yaonan and others to Beijing to appeal to the Ministry of Finance for cancellation. Due to the financial difficulties of merchants in Jiangsu, the salt transported by various transporters is piled up on ships and they are unwilling to transport it ashore to pay the surcharge. It is reported that the Ministry of Finance has telegraphed the Anhui provincial government ordering the cancellation. However, the newly established Anhui Provincial Defense Salt Tax Surcharge Northern Anhui Collection Bureau in Bengbu is mandated by the provincial government to collect the surcharge. A few days ago, it sent an official letter to the Bengbu General Chamber of Commerce and the Salt and Grain Guild, asking them to inform the merchants to quickly report to the bureau to pay the surcharge in order to issue tickets for release, stating that it was ordered by the Department of Finance and must be done immediately and that salt ships would not be released without the surcharge ticket issued by the bureau. (January 12)

Relief Issues After Abolishing Likin in Fujian Province 72

Provincial Government Asks Ministry of Finance for Financial Assistance

Fuzhou Communication: After Fujian Province was ordered to abolish likin, it abolished all taxes with the nature of transit tax, such as parcel tax, fertilizer tax, candle tax, brick and tile tax, cargo ship tax, and firewood and rice tax. The currently handled sugar, tea, bamboo, wood, oil, livestock, seafood, hardware, and various consumption taxes were also suspended. The Financial Special Envoy's Office began to handle the closure on January 1st and will implement the abolition on February 1st. However, after the abolition of the above taxes, the annual income will decrease by about five million yuan. Although the Department of Finance is preparing to implement a business tax to make up for it, it is currently uncertain how much revenue will be generated each month. In addition, various consumption taxes were originally designated for the military expenses of the national army stationed in Fujian. If the expenses of the national army are directly handled by the ministry in the future, how will they be paid? This has also become a major problem. Recently, the Department of Finance sent Secretary Director Shi Jialin and the Special Envoy's Office sent First Section Chief Zhang Zhedan to Shanghai to report to Yang Shuzhuang. Yang then sent Provincial Committee Members Zheng Baoqing and Lin Zhiyuan to Beijing with Shi and Zhang to discuss relief measures with the Ministry of Finance. It is reported that they have asked the Ministry of Finance to assist the province with 380,000 yuan per month during the transition period between the old and new taxes and to allocate 600,000 yuan at once to reimburse the advance payments of the abolished tax contracting agents. However, it is reported that the Ministry of Finance believes that after the business tax is levied in Fujian Province, it can generate about 400,000 yuan per month, and the difference is not much. It has only agreed to assist with 100,000 yuan per month. As for the one-time subsidy of 600,000 yuan, it is unable to pay due to the current financial difficulties of the national treasury and has ordered the provincial government to find its own way. Therefore, a satisfactory result has not been obtained. In addition, the salt tax surcharge in the province generates about 120,000 yuan per month, which is designated for the expenses of provincial schools. The Ministry of Finance has also decided to take it over into the national treasury from March 1st and has ordered to find other ways to make up for the educational expenses. On the 7th of this month, Education Department Director Cheng Shizhen convened a meeting with Education Expense Management Office Director Chen Peikun, Salt Commissioner Shen Qinmian, Audit Office Manager Cui Weide, and Finance Department Director He Gonggan, and decided that before the special education funds in the province are properly raised, the Salt Transport Office will temporarily invite merchants to contract the sale of upstream salt, which can generate more than 110,000 yuan per month, which will be allocated by the Audit Office to the Education Expense Management Office to maintain education. (January 9)

The Haiyuan Pavilion Library's Collection is Almost Entirely Lost 73

Wang Guanjun Caused the Most Damage During His Stationing in Liaocheng

The Yang Family Has Already Transported the Remaining Books to Jinan

Jinan Correspondence: The Yang family's Haiyuan Pavilion Library in Liaocheng County, Shandong (formerly Dongchang), is one of China's four most famous private book collections. The Yang family, over three generations, collected an extremely vast collection. There were no fewer than four or five hundred rare editions from the Song and Yuan dynasties, and with other scattered items, a total of more than two thousand types. This was extremely important to Chinese culture. Unfortunately, the Yang family's descendants did not know how to properly preserve them. Some were stolen and transported by troops, while others were sold to foreigners on their own. As of now, they have been almost entirely lost, causing Chinese cultural relics to flow into foreign hands. It is outrageous. This reporter recently went to Liaocheng to investigate the truth and inspect the garrison and bandit suppression situation in western Shandong. On the 11th, they departed from Jinan. After arriving in Liaocheng, they immediately went to inspect the Yang family's Haiyuan Pavilion. The Haiyuan Pavilion is located north of Guanjie Road in the county town. The buildings are very large and currently serve as the headquarters of the 87th Brigade Commander, Rong Guangxing. This reporter obtained permission from the army to enter and visit, and met with Chief of Staff Xie Yonglin. The Haiyuan Pavilion's book storage rooms totaled more than ten, but they are now completely empty, which was very unexpected. According to detailed investigation, during the Zhang Zongchang era, there was talk of nationalizing the Yang family's collection, so the descendants used cars to transport twenty-six types of rare books to Tianjin and subsequently sold them to foreigners. Last year, the bandit Guanjun entered and occupied Liaocheng, and the headquarters was set up in the Haiyuan Pavilion. This was the period of greatest destruction for the Yang family's collection. In addition to transporting a large number of books from the Yang family, Wang burned even more of them. He even used books to make fires for cooking, used books as mattresses for sleeping, used books to wipe guns and lamps when smoking opium, and used books to wipe tables and noses. He used books for everything, causing ancient books worth more than a dozen cities to be almost completely destroyed. He is truly the greatest criminal against Chinese culture. In November of last year, the 87th Brigade of the Third Route Army, led by Rong Guangxing, defeated the Wang bandits and recovered Liaocheng. In the city of Liaocheng, nine out of ten houses were empty. Not a single person was seen in the Yang residence. Books were scattered all over the yard, both inside and outside. There was no place in the toilet or stables where books were not found. The books in the yard were all soaked by heavy rain. However, inside the ten or so book storage rooms, the shelves were still full of books, but they were uneven and incomplete. The collection consisted mostly of manuscripts. Brigade Commander Rong knew that the Yang family's collection was important to Chinese culture, so Chief of Staff Xie Yonglin sent a company of soldiers to collect all the Yang family's books, regardless of whether they were complete, incomplete, or broken, and transport them into the house for safekeeping. No one was allowed to enter to view them in order to prevent further loss. Five days later, a nephew of the Yang family came to the brigade headquarters at the Haiyuan Pavilion to negotiate. He met with Xie Yonglin. This person's speech was very vulgar and he did not seem to be very literate. He said that the Commercial Press had once come to the residence to negotiate, offering 200,000 yuan to reprint part of the Haiyuan Pavilion's collection in order to preserve the secret texts, but the offer was rejected. Unexpectedly, the collection has now been ruined like this. A month later, on December 26th, the Yang family's nephew used dozens of carts to transport all the broken books to Jinan. Brigade Commander Rong also sent troops to protect the transportation, which took several days to complete. It is said that after being transported to Jinan, they were stored in the Yang family's own houses in Jianxingli, Weiyi Road. A total of six or seven large boxes were packed. The Yang family is still keeping it a secret, not wanting anyone to know. They are now building additional book storage houses in order to house the books. The person in charge of the Yang family is currently an old lady who has said to people that no matter what, she will do her best to preserve these books and not let them be lost, nor will she sell them. No matter who covets these books, she will resist with her life and not let them take a single one. As for the books sold in Tianjin, most of them were looted by the bandit army when they occupied Liaocheng. People have been sent to Tianjin to try to buy them back. It is also heard that the provincial government recently sent an order to Liaocheng, instructing Liaocheng County Magistrate Sun Tongfeng to investigate the Yang family's collection and preserve it. The old cultural power in Liaocheng is extremely strong, and it was most prosperous in the late Qing Dynasty. The county had three top scholars, one Grand Secretary, a thousand civil and military officials, and hundreds of scholars. To this day, they still adhere to ancient etiquette. The people all wear long robes, high collars, and thick white-soled shoes, like the Banner People of Beiping. Most of the women still bind their feet, and very few have unbound them. It is very difficult to instill new culture. The people hardly know what the party is. Every time a meeting is held, it is often delayed for five or six hours, or even not attended. There is the Provincial Third Normal School, the Second Middle School, and the Normal School Affiliated Elementary School, as well as two or three county-run elementary schools. The results are good, but the people of Liaocheng are ignorant and easily exploited by warlords and bandits. Xue Chuanfeng, Wang Jinfeng, and Wang Guanjun were able to cause trouble because of this. (13th)

Trial Record of the Liyang Land Tax Embezzlement Case 74

The Court is Scheduled to Announce the Verdict on the 31st

The Liyang Land Tax Embezzlement Case, after more than ten investigation hearings by the Zhenjiang Court, was finally prosecuted. The court was opened yesterday (14th). The content of the indictment generally states that the former Liyang Land Tax Director, Cai Hanyu, rebelled and was executed. At that time, the government affairs were suspended. The former County Magistrate Zhang Quan and the former Director of the Finance Bureau,

Page 11

Important News

Bin, along with the finance bureau staff, took the opportunity to steal a portion of the grain. They claimed it was lost during the Cai bandit rebellion. When the people were busy paying their taxes, they collected the taxes for their own private gain and colluded to embezzle. The approximate amount of embezzlement was over 40,000 yuan, which was divided among Zhang, Pan, and the staff at all levels. Later, Zhang Quan was dismissed and Zheng Chengyuan succeeded him. He knew about the embezzlement and intended to report it, but he was bribed with 6,000 yuan by people in the Finance Bureau to stop. Then, Education Bureau Director Ren Shuchun, Section Chief Di Hongzhu, County Party Committee Standing Committee members Shi Taorong, and secretaries Shi Qinglian and Hu Jinghua, as well as the Fourth District Chief Zhou Shi, learned about the situation one after another and also threatened to extort money. However, as the embezzlement continued for a long time, the staff of the Finance Bureau at all levels accused each other of unfair distribution of the loot, and scandalous rumors spread everywhere. Therefore, local people Wang Pingling and Zhou Bisheng filed a complaint with the provincial government. The provincial government detained Zheng Chengyuan and thirteen others for questioning and transferred them to the Zhenjiang Court for handling. The Procuratorate of the court found the investigation to be true and prosecuted them separately as follows: (1) For the land tax embezzlement part, the defendants were Zhang Quan, Pan Bin, Huang Xing'an, Shen Zhiqin, Zou Hanliang, Cheng Linshen, Zhou Ganqing, Chen Ronglin, Cao Qingzhi, Lu Zhiwen, Zhao Dianhua, etc., eleven people. (2) For the part of accepting bribes, Zheng Chengyuan. (3) For the part of extortion, Ren Shuchun, Di Hongxun, Shi Taorong, Shi Qinglian, Hu Jinghua, Zhou Shi, etc., six people.

The case was publicly tried yesterday (14th) starting at 10:00 AM. The plaintiffs who were summoned arrived, and the witnesses were Wang Pingling (Zhou Bisheng had a long-distance phone call to Zhen saying that he could not come to Zhen due to the river being frozen), Song Guangqian, Wu Jiabin, and Shi Guiguan. The defendants Zheng Chengyuan, Pan Bin, Huang Xing'an, Shen Zhiqin, Cao Qingzhi, Lu Zhiwen, Shi Taorong, Shi Qinglian, Hu Jinghua, Ren Shuchun, Di Hongxun, Zhou Shi, Zhao Dianhua, etc., a total of seventeen people. Judge Yang Changdi, together with two assessors Zhong Shicheng and Zhou Baochu, Prosecutor Yan Changtao, and Clerk Wu Zutai, ascended to the first criminal court. The defense lawyers who attended were Chen Liren representing Zheng Chengyuan, Jiang Shijie representing Pan Bin, Tao Rong representing Shen Zhiqin, and Zhu Fengen representing Cao Qingzhi, four people. However, because there were so many people who were summoned for questioning, the trial began at 10:00 AM and only finished at about 3:00 AM this morning (15th). The length of time spent set a new record for trials in the Zhenjiang court. The results of the trial were that Zhou Shi, Lu Zhiwen, and Zhao Dianhua were ordered to hand over the original guarantee, and Zheng Chengyuan, Di Hongxun, Ren Shuchun, etc., were ordered to pay additional cash bail. Because they were temporarily unable to afford it, they were ordered to be detained together with Pan Bin and others. Judge Yang announced that the verdict was scheduled to be announced at 2:00 PM on the 21st of this month. (15th)

Jinshan 75

Robbery and kidnapping cases at the end of the year and the beginning of the year: The southern part of this county has long been occupied by bandits. Recently, they have gathered more and more people, and their momentum is even more rampant. The recent kidnapping cases are summarized as follows: (1) In the Taojiaku area northeast of Langxia, the son of Tao Heshang, who is studying at a certain elementary school in the town, usually goes out early and returns late. Unexpectedly, on the way home after school the other day, he was kidnapped by the bandit Yang Meimei. Later, he was redeemed for 500 yuan. (2) Jin Sheng, the son of Luo Amao, north of Dashiqiao, was kidnapped by the bandit Xu Ximing (also known as tailor A Jin) the other day. The ransom demanded was very high. Because his family had no money to redeem him, he is still in the bandit's den. (3) Shen Huoquan, a farmer in the Nanmoku area north of Wanchun Bridge, was also kidnapped by the bandit Yang Meimei the other day. There has been no news of him so far. (4) The family of Gao Chuansheng, a farmer in the Luhetan area north of Zhangyan, had already been extorted by bandits several times. Unexpectedly, on the night of December 30th, many armed bandits came again, led by the bandit leader Xu Ximing. They first robbed and then kidnapped his four-month-old son, hiding him in the home of a bandit named Xiao in the Chianxu southeast Chang'an area. Later, Qiu Awu was asked to negotiate, and finally he was redeemed for 1,040 yuan. (5) Yang Zhaohe's family in the Cao'an area southeast of Baziqiao received a threatening letter from the bandits on December 29th, demanding a bandit payment of 1,000 yuan. Zhaohe ignored it. Unexpectedly, on January 1st, several bandits came again and took Zhaohe's wife away. Later, people were asked to intercede, and finally she was redeemed for 100 yuan. (6) On the evening of January 5th, more than twenty bandits suddenly came to several houses in the Kongjiaque northwest Danzhu area, including Zhu Wuxiang and Zhu Ruizhi. They robbed people in the house. Wuxiang's wife, who was 67 years old, was shot in a vital part by the bandits and died. They also wanted to kidnap Wuxiang's son Dajie, but fortunately he had crossed the river to escape. However, Ruizhi's son was unable to escape and was tied up by the bandits. Later, his servant escaped and sounded the alarm. He was released halfway. When the Kongjiaque Security Corps heard the alarm and pursued, the bandits had already fled.

Nanhui 76

A Steamer Disaster in Chuannan Due to Carelessness: The Chuannan scheduled steamer was about to leave Zhugiao Town yesterday when it was heading to Chuansha. Because the water pipe was frozen and could not be started, the mechanic poured cold water to heat it up to unfreeze it. Unexpectedly, due to carelessness, a fire broke out immediately. Although they tried their best to put out the fire, the fire was very fierce, causing most of the ship's top and cabin to be burned down. Fortunately, all the passengers were safe.

Too Light a Punishment for the Death of an Athlete: At the end of last year, the county government received a letter from the Shanghai Education Bureau, stating that Yu Zhenhua, a student of Tonghui Elementary School, had been borrowed by Zhoupu Elementary School to participate in the Nanhui County Elementary and Secondary School Games. Due to continuous strenuous exercise, he contracted an illness and died. After investigation, it was found to be true. In addition to severely punishing Tonghui Elementary School as a warning, they requested that the principals and teachers of the Zhoupu Elementary School be severely punished. The county government then transferred the order to the Education Bureau for follow-up. According to the bureau's report, it was decided to suspend the physical education teacher Cai Fei's teaching qualification for two years. The county government considered the punishment to be too light and specially instructed the bureau yesterday to discuss a stricter punishment in order to set an example.

Suzhou 77

Arrest of the Remnants of the Haizhou Gang: Yi Xuan, the leader of the eleventh team of the third district of the water police, received a report from a secret agent on the morning of the 14th, saying that Lu Fashan, a remnant of the Haizhou Gang leader Zhang Zhaohua, who had already been executed, was hiding in the Xujiawan area outside Fengmen, opening a hall to accept apprentices. Team Leader Pei immediately led the team and captured the Lu bandit in the Xinyuan teahouse in the village. He immediately took the Lu bandit to his home to search, and found a lot of stolen goods such as gold jewelry and clothes. Then he escorted Lu back to the team for a brief interrogation. According to the confession, he robbed, kidnapped and extorted money in Zhangyan, Zhangpu, Longwangmiao and other places. After hearing the confession, Team Leader Pei immediately sent him to the district office to await disposal.

More than 200 Political Prisoners Eligible for Amnesty: The Higher Court handled the amnesty. Yesterday (15th), the first, second, and third criminal court judges Lin Dawen and Zheng Chi sent more than 200 political prisoners who met the amnesty regulations to the review committee for review.

Reorganization of the General Chamber of Commerce: The reorganization of the Suzhou General Chamber of Commerce into the Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce has been in preparation for half a year. It was established yesterday (15th). A total of 58 guilds and 47 shops joined. The members' representative meeting was held in the morning, with 257 people actually present. Shi Yunqing was publicly elected as the chairman. After the meeting was held as usual, the articles of association were adopted and proposals were discussed. In the afternoon, voting was held. As a result, Shi Yunqing, Pang Tiansheng, Song Youpei, Luo Yanting, Xu Juebo, Zhang Yunbo, Pan Ziqi, Xu Xiaozhai, Wu Jiesheng, Lu Baoyu, Zhang Fuzhi, Xu Juesheng, Zhu Renan, Zhan Qigao, and Xu Kunquan were elected as executive members. There were also three alternate members, seven supervisors, and three alternate supervisors. By 7:00 PM, the vote counting had not yet been completed. It was also decided that the executive committee would hold its first meeting on the 20th of this month to mutually elect the standing committee and the presidium.

Wuxi 78

Opening of the County Administrative Conference: The second county administrative conference of this county was held in the county government hall at 10:30 AM yesterday (15th). Thirty to forty members attended. The formal meeting was held at 1:00 PM, electing the vice chairman, determining the seating order of the members, and the chairman appointed the reviewers of each group to hold a review meeting. The meeting adjourned after the discussion. The meeting will continue today to discuss various proposals.

Jiangyin Communist Leader Arrested in Wuxi: Jiangyin Communist leader Na Jincai has repeatedly committed major cases of murder, arson, kidnapping, extortion, and rape of women in the countryside of the county. Recently, the suspect fled to Wuxi and hid in the workshop of the Shenxin Yarn Factory outside Ximen. The Jiangyin Security Corps learned of this the other day and secretly sent investigator Miao Luncai to Wuxi to assist the county police in arresting him at his address. They captured Na Jincai and took him to the police headquarters for detention overnight. He was escorted back to Jiangyin yesterday to be tried.

Exhumation for Re-examination of the Lu Xiang Murder Case: Wang, the wife of Lu Bendada, a villager in Lu Xiang, 131st map of the Nan Shuangmiaoqiao West Township in the 15th District, suddenly died on the night of December 18th last year. Later, Liang, the investigator, went to the countryside to examine the body and determined that she had died from a blood burst. Wang Jiangshi, the mother of Lu Wang, believed that the examination was not true and filed a petition with the Higher Court requesting that someone be sent to Wuxi for re-examination to redress the grievance. Recently, the county government reported the examination situation to the High Court for instructions. After receiving the report, President Lin ordered the Procuratorate of the Wuxian District Court to appoint Prosecutor Lu Wenqin, accompanied by three clerks, to come to Wuxi by car from Suzhou the other day to meet with County Magistrate Pan, review the file, and instruct the political police Liu Yirong and others to go to the countryside first to investigate and summon the plaintiff Wang Jiangshi and Tupizheng Zhang Keji to gather at the corpse field for questioning. Yesterday at noon, Prosecutor Lu and others took a car to the countryside to carry out an exhumation for re-examination to clarify the truth.

Breach of Contract for Packaged Coal Causes Factory Shutdown: The silk factories in Xiyi have always signed long-term contracts with coal dealers for the coal used to burn, and they abide by each other. However, the coal used by the Nanqiao Shengyu Silk Factory, the Wugiao Xia Wansheng No. 1 Factory, the Yaoyao Wan Wansheng No. 2 Factory, and the Nantai Jintai Ruifu Taifu and other seven silk factories were all packaged by the Shanghai Lin Coal Company and a contract was signed. Recently, the company refused to deliver the coal due to soaring coal prices, causing the seven silk factories including Shengyu to have no coal to burn and unable to start their machines. Tens of thousands of workers are unemployed for no reason. In addition to hiring lawyers to carry out legal relief separately, the factories jointly sent a letter to the silk factory industry association yesterday, requesting that a meeting be convened to unanimously support them.

Zhenjiang 79

Construction Bonds Lottery: The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Bonds, previously approved by the Central Government, issued 7 million yuan. The first phase of 4 million yuan, from August 1, 1930, to January 31, 1931, was the first period for repayment of principal. The Finance Department specially scheduled to execute the lottery in public at the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 PM on the 15th of this month, and submitted a preliminary request to the provincial government to send personnel to jointly handle the lottery for the settlement of the Jiangsu Post-Disaster Old Bonds, and telegraphed the Ministry of Finance and the Audit Yuan to send personnel to monitor.

Organization of the Heritage Teaching Association Not Allowed: The Jiangsu Provincial Party Police Association, upon the request of Dongtai Taoist Zhu Benxing and others to organize a Taoist association, specially forwarded it to the Central Training Department for clarification. Yesterday, a directive was received from the Central Training Department, which stated that Chinese Taoists often use sutras, spells, and incantations to deceive people and the world, without clear doctrines or profound teachings, and are purely a kind of superstition. The request to organize a Taoist association should not be permitted. After receiving the order, the Provincial Rectification Committee, in addition to ordering the Dongtai County Party Department to comply, also issued a notice to all county party departments to comply.

Danyang 80

Detailed Record of the Bandit Police Incident in Wu Jiaqiao: More than one hundred bandits suddenly came to Wu Jiaqiao in the northern part of this county at about 3:00 AM on the night of the 5th of this month. They were wearing military uniforms and plain clothes, and about half of them were armed with fear guns, short guns, and hand grenades. They suddenly surrounded the police team stationed there and set fire to it. The policemen bravely rushed out and repelled the bandits. It is reported that the bandits also went to the homes of farmers such as Zhu Buqing that night, looting and burning. Wu Jiaqiao Township Chief Wang Bingsheng urgently sent someone to the city to report. The county government immediately ordered the police team leader Sun Longxun to transfer the entire team of cavalry and infantry to rush to suppress them, and also consulted with the Danyang Gendarmerie Company to send a team to join the suppression. When the county police team rushed to Guolonggang, about two miles away from Wu Jiaqiao, the bandits had not yet retreated. The police team immediately advanced and attacked. After about an hour, the bandits could not resist and began to retreat to the north. At that time, the gendarmerie also arrived, and the gendarmerie defended the rear, and the police team led the troops to pursue to the foot of the mountain north of Wu Jiaqiao. The bandits dispersed into the mountains to the northeast. This time, the third class of the second team of the police team originally stationed in Wu Jiaqiao was surrounded by bandits. Due to the small number of police and the large number of bandits, they were outnumbered. The injured included squad leader Yao Hongbin, deputy squad leader Xu Chuntang, policemen Cao Zuofa, Huang Ruiqing, and cook Yong Dengwu. Another policeman, Li Shouzheng, was seriously injured and burned to death when the bandits set fire to the station. It was also heard that the police team had captured three bandits, Xu Fuyin, Jiang Laoda, and Zou Qiaolin, while pursuing them in the countryside, and they are currently being interrogated.

Yangzhou 81

The Progress of Resolving Sun Jingtai's Troops: Since Sun Jingtai's troops were reorganized into the New Twenty-Seventh Division, they have often engaged in illegal activities in the Shuyang area of northern Jiangsu. Zhang Zhijiang, the Pacification Supervisor of Jiangsu, has received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek, ordering that the troops be resolved as soon as possible. The Governor's Office received a telegram from Chief Commander Liang Yuan yesterday morning (13th), reporting on the progress of resolving Sun's troops. The outline is as follows: (1) All departments followed the order and reached the designated locations on the day of the document, but when I approached Shuyang, the bandits had already detected it in advance and withdrew from the city, preparing to resist. Later, seeing the strength of my army, they rushed out of the encirclement in the northeast direction. They were severely attacked by the Liu and Wang brigades, and the bandits fled in all directions. A total of three regiments were resolved, many bandits were killed, more than 300 were captured, more than 100 guns, one mountain gun, two mortars, more than 100 horses, one bandit battalion commander Diao Damin, two battalion commanders, and the entire repair shop were captured. Sun led the remnants and fled to Fangshan Street. (2) The other departments all had captures and are currently being cleared. (3) Most of the bandits are hiding in the city and scattered in the countryside. Liu, the brigade commander, has been appointed as the city defense commander to conduct a thorough search. The brigade is stationed near the city. (4) Sun Fengxiang, the brigade commander of the First Cavalry Division, was ordered to lead the team through Rouxu, Fangshan, and Yangfu Street, and Wu Tianbin, the deputy division commander of the Third Cavalry Division, was ordered to lead the team through Houzhentou, all to pursue in the direction of the Longhai Railway. They were all limited to passing through the railway and informed the Jin and Han division commanders to send teams to intercept. (5) The Wang brigade was gathered near Xiaojie, and the Zheng brigade was gathered near Shiziqiao. (6) Subsequent actions, and the disposition of the troops left in Shuyang and the prisoners, are requested to be indicated for compliance. It is heard that Zhang Wei, the division and brigade commander, Cheng Quanfu, the staff officer, and Xue Gaoliang, the adjutant, are still being detained in the Governor's Office.

Hangzhou 82

Statistics on the Amount of Imported Kerosene: The amount of kerosene imported into Zhejiang Province has increased year by year. According to statistics from the Department of Construction, the imported gasoline, paraffin oil, and refined oil totaled 100.26 million gallons, with a value of 56.127 customs taels. The imported kerosene totaled 108.20196 million gallons, with a value of 1,833,392 customs taels. The imported lubricating oil totaled 196,309 gallons, with a value of 700,065 customs taels. The imported diesel totaled 2.292 tons, with a value of 174,575 customs taels. The imported paraffin totaled 14,340 dan, with a value of 181,242 customs taels. The imported asphalt totaled 6 dan, with a value of 14 customs taels. The total value of imports for the year was 30,216,001 customs taels.

Ancient Wood Discovered in the Reservoir Excavation: Since the Preparatory Committee for Waterworks in Hangzhou began excavating and building the reservoir outside Qintai Gate, many ancient porcelain, shells, and ancient animals have been discovered. The other day, many ancient trees were suddenly discovered in the area being excavated, about thirty to forty trees. The longer ones were dug to more than ten feet, but they have not been pulled out yet. The matter was heard by the museum, which sent a letter to send personnel to negotiate. Several sections have been taken to the museum for display. It has been said that they are pine trees from the Han Dynasty.

Ningbo 83

Planned Organization of Post-Abolition Municipal Affairs Group: Ningbo City has been ordered to be abolished by the provincial government and is about to end. Citizens Fan Chunjin, Wang Lijia, and others from the urban area believe that since the municipal government has been abolished, municipal construction will be suspended with great difficulty. Although the province has resolved to hand over management to the Yin County Magistrate, they fear that he may not be able to handle it adequately. Therefore, they plan to organize a municipal affairs post-abolition group in advance to handle municipal affairs after the official abolition of the municipal government. The method is to first gather fair and just gentry in the city to send a telegram to the province stating the reasons for the organization. This organization is currently under negotiation and is expected to become a reality soon.

Kidnapping Cases in Eastern and Western Yin County: At the Wan Shun Rice Store in Miao Jiaqiao, eastern Yin County, around 12 o'clock the night before, seven or eight robbers suddenly broke into the store, each wielding sharp weapons. They injured Chen Azeng, the store's business manager, in the head, resulting in an estimated loss of over one hundred yuan. Also, Chen Meidi, a resident of Qiaotou, Yuanzhen Bridge in western Yin County, is only sixteen years old and already married. He has a seventy-year-old grandmother and wife, totaling four family members. Meidi is currently studying at the people's night school run by Yuanzhen Bridge Primary School. Unexpectedly, around 9 o'clock the night before, when he returned home after school and was knocking on the door, he was suddenly kidnapped by robbers who had been lying in wait outside the door. By the time his grandmother opened the door, Meidi was gone. The next day, the robbers sent a letter demanding 5,000 yuan for ransom. It is said that Meidi's family only has a meager twenty-odd acres of land, and even if they sold everything they own, they would not be able to raise 5,000 yuan.

Ten Thousand Yuan in Banknotes Suddenly Turns into Tinfoil: On the Yongchuan ship sailing between Wenzhou and Haimen, the previous trip involved the Yuanyou Money Exchange in Wenzhou entrusting the transportation of 10,000 yuan in silver dollars to the Yongfeng Money Exchange in Haimen. These silver dollars were entrusted to Zhu Yousheng, a staff member of the ship, to be taken to Haimen. When Zhu handed over the silver dollars entrusted by Yuanyou, the Yongfeng Exchange opened the package and found that it had turned into tinfoil, causing great surprise. The exchange immediately questioned Zhu, but Zhu refused to take responsibility because the package was intact. It is reported that legal solutions are now being pursued.

Fengxian 84

Investigation by the Construction Bureau Regarding the Nanting River Project: After Zhuang Tianmei, Xu Yizhou, and others filed a complaint regarding the Nanting River project's financial report, the county government, together with the Construction Bureau, conducted an investigation. Due to their lax supervision, the two directors, one in the east and one in the west, were each given a major demerit on record. Now, Zhuang and others believe that the county's handling is too lenient, so they have sent representatives to the province to petition, and have extracted various clauses from the River Project Review Committee as evidence of corruption. Because the Construction Bureau believes that the case has been causing disturbances for a long time, they summoned Zhou Jiuxu, the director of the Construction Bureau, the day before yesterday for questioning. The day before yesterday, they also ordered the county to summon the former directors of the eastern and western river projects, namely Jiang Rongchu and Zhang Fengtai, the chiefs of the first and eighth districts, to the province for verification. The bureau also dispatched a special commissioner yesterday to Fengxian to retrieve various contract documents and other items related to the river project, stating that they would be handed over to an accountant for item-by-item review in order to thoroughly investigate the matter.

Difficulties in the Transfer of Funds and Property of Charitable Halls: Although the old and new preparatory committees of the local Relief Institute have already completed the handover, the funds and property of various charitable halls that should be taken over have not been fully received. The new preparatory committee discussed this issue the other day and decided to issue a warning first. If they still refuse to comply, the county will enforce the law to clear the matter up. However, it is now known that the charitable halls believe that there are no provisions in the ministry's orders regarding changes or reorganizations of the original charitable funds and property, so most advocate maintaining the status quo, leading to disputes and each side sticking to its own position, making it unlikely that the issue will be resolved in a short period of time. Unauthorized Decapitation Results in Major Demerit from the Provincial Government: The Ministry of Civil Affairs has given Yang Xingsheng, the captain of the second police squad of the county, a major demerit because on December 3rd of last year, he killed the bandit Xiao Gang at the home of Cao Qinghe in Niuqiao Township, and then, without following regulations, arbitrarily decapitated and displayed the head. The ministry considered this a violation of law and discipline, so it issued a major demerit and reprimanded him the day before yesterday. As for the key suspect, Tang Yixin, who was captured by the squad for burning and looting in Zhuanghang, he is still being detained in the county jail pending verification, as the province has not yet sent a reply to the county.

Shaoxing 85

Butchers Request Permission to Inflate and Remove Hair: Butchers in Shaoxing are finding it difficult because the Silk Administration prohibits inflating to remove hair. They have repeatedly requested that the order be withdrawn, but their requests have not been approved. Currently, there are more pig slaughters below each butcher shop. On the 13th, the 47 shops together sent representatives to petition the county government. The county government told them that inflating to remove hair is related to hygiene and ordered them to gradually improve their methods before dispersing.

Important News

Ministry of Education's Reform Work 86

丨December of the 19th Year丨

The Ministry of Education's December Reform Work Report for the 19th year has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for record and reported to various internal divisions.

(1) Higher Education

(1) Investigation of Party Ideology Teachers and Guidance Directors: A notice was issued to colleges and universities to submit survey forms on the general situation of Party Ideology teachers and guidance directors. (2) Restrictions on Funding for Government-Sponsored Students Studying Abroad: A notice was issued to education departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities that in the future, when sending government-sponsored students to study abroad, they must have funds and declare that they have no outstanding debts before being approved for study abroad certificates. (3) Expediting the Application for Special Permission from the Judicial Yuan for Private Political and Legal Schools: An order was sent to the education bureaus of Shanghai and Peiping to instruct schools that were approved for establishment after the promulgation of the regulations on special permission from the Judicial Yuan for private political and legal schools in April of this year to apply for special permission from the Judicial Yuan in accordance with the regulations. (4) Registration of Private Colleges: An order was sent to the Nanjing Education Bureau to approve the registration of the private Ginling Women's Arts and Sciences College. An order was sent to the Shanghai Education Bureau to approve the registration of the private Shanghai Law College. (5) Issuance of Study Abroad Certificates: Approved for the issuance of government-sponsored study abroad certificates to a total of five people: one to the UK, one to the US, and three to Japan. Approved for the issuance of self-funded study abroad certificates to a total of eighty-six people: three to the UK, six to the US, three to Germany, ten to France, five to Belgium, and fifty-nine to Japan.

(2) Secondary Education

(1) List of Registered Secondary Schools in December:

Zhenheng Junior High School (Jiangsu), Jianghuai Junior High School (Anhui), Daxia University Affiliated Middle School (Shanghai), Xiuye Agricultural School (Hunan), Guide Normal School Board of Directors (Rehe), Aimei Junior High School (Shandong), Yuying Junior High School (Shandong). (2) Defining Uniform Measures for Secondary School Names. (3) Completion of Provisional Standards for Normal School Courses (For Printing). (4) Defining the Reporting Form for Secondary Schools. (5) An order was issued to education departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities to handle the acceptance of transfer students in accordance with Article 18 of the Provisional Regulations for Middle Schools, without the need to establish separate restrictions.

(3) Elementary Education

(1) Jointly with the Capital Construction Committee and the Nanjing Education Bureau, drafted measures for the construction of elementary school buildings in the capital. (2) An order was issued to the Commercial Press to immediately cease the publication of the unrevised version of the New Learning Elementary School Industrial Arts Textbook. (3) Statistics on Moral Education Items and Moral Education Standards for Elementary Schools.

(4) Overseas Chinese Education

(1) List of Registered Overseas Chinese Schools in December: Yihua Overseas Chinese School (British Penang), Jugang Chinese School (Dutch Jugang), Jugang Overseas Chinese School (Same as above), Baoping Yili School (British Singapore), Zhongshan Overseas Chinese School (Honolulu), Diwen Lieli Chinese School (Portuguese South Ocean). (2) Revised the Regulations of the Overseas Chinese School Teacher Introduction Center.

(5) Matters Concerning Local Education Administration

(1) Appointed Xu Peihuang as the Director of the Shanghai Education Bureau. (2) An order was sent to the Shandong Provincial Education Department that vocational schools must be planned in their entirety, those that have been suspended should be quickly restored, and those that are currently operating should be vigorously expanded. (3) An order was sent to the Shanghai Education Bureau to pay attention to the Education Committee of the Municipal Council at all times. If the Council's measures conflict with our country's laws or infringe on sovereignty, they should vigorously negotiate and report to the Ministry. (4) It was agreed with the Ministry of Finance that 20% of the proceeds from the sale of official land in Zhejiang Province should be used for education expenses and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval.

(6) Social Education

(1) Issued the 18th Year Social Education Survey Statistics Form. (2) Issued a Small Booklet for Learning Phonetic Symbols. (3) Prohibited the illegal almanac printed by Hu Shunxing's Astronomical Room in Wenzhou, Zhejiang. (4) Banned the reactionary publication "Oriental Daily". (5) Issued the 20th Year National Almanac in Han and Mongolian. (6) Consulted the Ministry of Interior to request the Capital Police Department to uniformly add phonetic symbols to the street and alley nameplates in the capital. (7) Telegraphed various universities to urge all faculty, staff, and students to complete the study of phonetic symbols before the winter vacation so that they could teach them when they return to their hometowns during the vacation. (8) Consulted the Shandong Provincial Government to protect the ancient relics and artifacts of Dai Temple in Tai'an and to properly draft repair and protection measures. (9) Submitted to the Executive Yuan to request the Xinjiang Provincial Government to immediately send personnel to strictly investigate Stein's new work objectives. If there are violations of orders, the originally issued passport and the obtained antiques should be confiscated and he should be ordered to leave the country.

(7) Mongolian and Tibetan Education

(1) Placement of Mongolian and Tibetan Students: Sent a letter to the Executive Yuan Secretariat regarding the Xikang student Huang Qiguang, etc., who have now been sent to study in the Mongolian and Tibetan Local Autonomy Class of the Central Political School. The Ministry has also sent the student's certificates and photos to the Xikang Office for forwarding to the student. (2) Progress of Mongolian and Tibetan Schools: The West Mongolian and Tibetan Committee requested the compilation of budget estimates for the Nanjing and Kangding Mongolian and Tibetan Schools so that they could be submitted to the Executive Yuan for early approval.

(8) Formulation, Review, and Interpretation of Education Laws and Regulations

(1) Ordered the rectification of academic atmosphere. (2) Ordered the issuance of President Jiang, who concurrently serves as the Premier of the Executive Yuan, to issue an ancient warning letter to students nationwide, and ordered compliance. (3) Notified the key points of the organization of student groups in elementary schools. (4) Notified that provincial supervisors should be treated as section chiefs with the rank of recommended appointment. (5) Notified that the revenue from temple sale certificates donated to schools may be given certificates of merit in accordance with the regulations on rewarding private groups for donating to establish schools under Article 2. (6) Notified that student self-government associations in schools under the jurisdiction of provinces should be managed separately by cities and counties, and their charters do not need to be submitted to the Provincial Education Department for approval. (7) Submitted to the Executive Yuan that Liu Heng and four others have donated more than 30,000 yuan to establish schools, and requested that the National Government be notified to commend them in accordance with the regulations at the end of the year. (8) Sorted out the draft Elementary School Organization Law. (9) Sorted out the draft Middle School Organization Law.

(9) Education Statistics

(1) Creation of a map showing the location of secondary and higher education institutions nationwide. (2) Created a statistical table summarizing the national university situation in the 17th year. (3) Created various forms for reporting matters for secondary schools. (4) Managed a summary report of statistical work from June to December.

Ministry of Education Submits to the Central Government for Swift Approval of the National Education Reform Plan 87

The ten chapters of the National Education Reform Plan resolved at the Second National Education Conference include concrete measures for improving education at all levels. After the entire plan was resolved, the Ministry of Education submitted it to the Executive Yuan of the National Government for forwarding to the Central Political Conference for approval so that it could be implemented separately based on the plan. Because it has been a long time and it has not yet been approved and promulgated, the Ministry of Education submitted a request to the Executive Yuan yesterday (the 14th) for forwarding to the National Government to urge the Central Political Conference to quickly approve and issue the plan so that it can serve as the basis for improving national education. The original submission stated: "The National Education Reform Plan resolved at the Second National Education Conference was submitted to your esteemed Yuan in June of last year for forwarding to the National Government, and the department has also submitted it to the Central Political Conference for review. Currently, this plan has not yet been approved and promulgated, and all the department's measures for improving national education are pending this basis. Therefore, we are submitting a document to request your esteemed Yuan to forward it to the National Government for review and to forward it to the Central Political Conference for prompt review and promulgation so that it can be followed."

Local News

Municipal Education Bureau Orders That Graduates of Unregistered Private Schools May Not Serve as Elementary School Teachers 89

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued a directive to municipal elementary schools yesterday, stating, "It has been found that this Bureau previously, in accordance with Article 28 of the Regulations for Private Schools, 'Students and graduates of unregistered private schools may not receive the same treatment as students of registered schools.' Also, the Regulations for Specialized Schools and the Regulations for Universities stipulate that 'Students of unregistered private schools may not transfer to public or registered private schools.' Regarding whether the employment of graduates of unregistered private schools as teachers in various schools should be prohibited, the Ministry of Education issued Directive No. 36, which stated, 'The report has been noted. It has been found that there are many graduates of normal schools in Shanghai and nearby areas. Elementary schools should select teachers based on qualifications. Graduates of unregistered private schools may not be employed as elementary school teachers unless they have passed a qualification examination. Those who have already been approved for registration by the Bureau but have not yet been formally examined should be checked and distinguished at any time. Those who have not yet been registered should not be registered again in order to emphasize teacher qualifications and prevent malpractice.' This directive, and others, must be complied with. In addition to those who have already been approved for registration and should be subject to inspection and assessment at any time, we hereby order all elementary schools in the city to comply."

Chinese Chemical Industry Association Visits Zhenhua Paint Manufacturing Factory 90

The Chinese Chemical Industry Association held its annual meeting at the beginning of the new year and visited the Zhenhua Paint Company's manufacturing factory. The members first gathered at the company's distribution office at Tianhou Temple Bridge on North Suzhou Road. Over forty people attended, including Cao Huiqun, Xu Huang, Hu Shuhua, Wu Yun Chu, Xu Mingcai, Chen Guangshun, etc. They rode in automobiles to the factory on Zhongshan Road in Zhabei, where they were received and guided by Manager Shao Jinqing. They visited the heavy paint department, blending paint department, varnish department, improved gold paint department, enamel department, oil boiling department, oil bleaching department, pigment department, red lead department, testing laboratory, raw material warehouse, and finished product warehouse. The buildings were grand, and the layout was well-organized. After the tour, the company hosted a luncheon at the Dajiali Restaurant. The factory director, Su Lizhai, gave a welcoming speech and mentioned the difficulties in not being able to fully use domestic raw materials. Then, Hu Shuhua and Xu Peihuang gave speeches on the need to actively promote domestic industry and commerce and to improve various aspects, which were quite insightful. The guests and hosts happily dispersed at three o'clock.
