Regulations for Parking on Hongqiao Road 121

Joint Announcement by the Municipal Public Works Bureau and Public Security Bureau

Announcement by the Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau and Public Security Bureau: Regarding the joint announcement, according to a report from the Chief of the First Station of the Sixth District of the Public Security Bureau, the foreign and Chinese residents in this port are mixed, and there is a mix of good and bad. Recently, cases of kidnapping have been repeatedly reported in both the Chinese and Foreign Concessions. The only tool used by kidnappers is often automobiles. The police have a special responsibility to maintain public safety and prevent and arrest kidnappers. Therefore, your honor instructed each district and station to set up checkpoints to inspect passing cars and pedestrians during the last business meeting, which is an excellent way to eliminate bandits. After implementing the order, it has been effective. For example, as reported on November 9, the case of Chai Renji stealing wood is clear evidence. It has been found that the Hongqiao Road area under my jurisdiction is a remote area in western Shanghai and a frequent route for Chinese and foreign travelers. Passengers often abandon their cars on the roadside for five or six hours, or even all day, without driving them away. The police often mistakenly believe these are the cars of kidnappers, searching everywhere, worried all day. After clarifying the identity of the person in the car, they say they went to a banquet somewhere or hunting in the distance. The car owner only needs to make a brief statement to safely retrieve the car. The police, with the duty to protect the people, dare not complain about their labor in searching all day. However, car owners arbitrarily abandoning their cars on the roadside not only easily leads to misunderstandings and obstructs traffic but also violates police regulations and cannot avoid punishment. It is proposed that your bureaus jointly announce to all car owners that, hereafter, when parking on Hongqiao Road in western

Page 16

Shanghai, drivers must remain in the car to wait. If questioned by police officers, they must immediately present their licenses for inspection. This method will not cause any difficulty for passengers and will clearly distinguish between good and bad, effectively protecting the people. If, after the announcement, there are still those who do not comply, the responsible district and station are authorized to detain the case and punish them according to law, to serve as a warning and maintain public safety. Is this appropriate? We hereby submit a written request for your approval and compliance. In accordance with this, the Public Security Bureau has consulted with the Public Works Bureau and decided on measures to be taken for compliance. In addition to reporting to the Municipal Government for record, the following measures are listed below, announced for general knowledge, and must be obeyed without violation. This is the announcement. The measures for prohibiting parking on Hongqiao Road in western Shanghai are as follows: 1. When private cars are parked in the Hongqiao area, a driver must remain in the car. If the car owner is driving himself, someone must also stay to watch the car. When questioned by the police, all licenses must be presented for inspection immediately. 2. When commercial cars are parked in the Hongqiao area, a driver must remain to wait. If questioned by the police, all licenses must be presented for inspection. 3. Temporary parking areas must not obstruct traffic. 4. Violations of the above measures will be punished according to regulations. January of the twentieth year of the Republic of China. Director of the Public Works Bureau, Huang Boqiao. Director of the Public Security Bureau, Yuan Liang.

Hu Fuzhang's Mental Illness Problem 123

Hu Aji's son, Hu Fuzhang, a Chinese constable No. 526 of the Hongkou police station, on the evening of September 30 last year, held a kitchen knife in front of his house at No. 187 Chang Kang Li, Alabaster Road, intending to kill his birth mother, Ms. Ma. His father turned him over to the police station and sent him to the Special District Local Court. According to his father and others, Hu Fuzhang suffered from mental illness and was sent for medical examination. The Western doctor of the Municipal Council and the forensic doctor of the court came to different conclusions after examining him. The Western doctor of the Municipal Council said that he did not have any mental illness, while the forensic doctor of the Special Court said that he was suffering from mental illness. As a result, the judge did not know what to do and could not interrogate him, and ordered him to be examined in detail and reported again for review. Now, Wang Changlai, the Western doctor of the Municipal Council, has written a report to the Special Court on the condition of Hu Fuzhang's examination. The report stated: "Hu Fuzhang was sent to the Chinese Constable Hospital of the Municipal Council by the Huishi Police Station on November 12, 19th year of the Republic of China, on the order of your court. The doctor personally examined him every day and instructed the on-duty nurses to closely monitor all his actions and interactions with others. On November 25th, he was transferred to the Municipal Council Prison Hospital for continued examination. However, during the fourteen days that the defendant was in the Chinese Constable Hospital, the doctor's examination, the nurses' reports, and the discussions of the other inmates all proved that the defendant was no different from ordinary people. Now, according to the certificates of Zhou Liangquan and other two doctors of the Municipal Council Prison Hospital and the results of the doctor's examination, it has been determined that the defendant has not shown any signs of mental illness. This is the certificate." Another report from Zhou Liangquan and other two doctors of the Municipal Council Prison Hospital stated: "We have examined the prisoner Hu Fuzhang at the Municipal Council Prison Hospital from November 25, 19th year of the Republic of China, to January 9th of this year. During this period, the prisoner has not shown any signs of mental illness." Yesterday morning, the police sent the defendant to the Special Court to request a continued hearing. However, the court did not have an examination report and was still unable to proceed. Judge Wu briefly questioned the defendant, and according to Hu, he was hospitalized for two months, and the doctor only came to see him once every seven or ten days. He had a seizure in the hospital on December 22 last year, but the doctor did not know about it, etc. Judge Wu ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the hearing for the 20th of this month.

Emergency Meeting of the Firefighting Federation 124

Report from the Family of Liu Rongtai

Outlining the Attention of the Railway Bureau and Police Bureau

The Zhabei District Firefighting Federation, due to the death of Liu Rongtai, director of the Third Section Fire Brigade, who was fatally injured by a train while heading out to fight a fire, held an emergency meeting at 2 PM yesterday (the 15th). Those present included Yao Xiangsheng, director of the First Section, Yu Tingkai, director of the Second Section, Chen Jinxiang, acting director of the Third Section, member Chen Weihan, Federation staff Xu Youtang, Jin Shiru, and dozens of others. Chairman Wang Binyan presided over the meeting, conducting the formalities. First, Liu Minsheng, a family member of Liu, reported on the tragic death of Liu Rongtai, stating that at 10:47 PM on the 9th of this month, a fire broke out at You Jinji Cotton Factory, No. 286 Minli Road, Zhabei. Liu Rongtai rushed to the scene in his own car to provide assistance. At the railroad tracks on Gonghe Xin Road, a Shanghai-Hangzhou train was coming to Shanghai, and Liu Rongtai stopped to wait (there was only one gate leaf left at the four-leaf gate, and there was no red light). After the Shanghai-Hangzhou train passed, Liu Rongtai started to drive forward. Unexpectedly, the delayed No. 22 Beijing-Shanghai train arrived. The light from the headlight of the locomotive was not illuminating. Liu Rongtai did not see the light, and since the previous train had just passed and the sound of the wheels was still present, he did not suspect that another train was coming. He was violently hit, and the car was thrown dozens of yards. The train continued on its way, ignoring the incident. Moreover, there was supposed to be a guard booth next to the gate, but the guard also turned a blind eye. Later, the road police called the Central Fire Brigade in the Concession, who transferred the call to the Shenjiawan Fire Brigade. A Western staff member from the brigade, Mr. Henry, and a companion came in a car from the Henan Road Fire Brigade to investigate. However, because the car did not have a Chinese Concession license, it could not enter. They walked to the scene of the accident and identified it as Liu Rongtai. At that time, the wind and snow were severe, and the temperature was below 14 degrees. Liu Rongtai was already covered in several inches of snow. Mr. Henry tried to carry Liu Rongtai into the trackman's room next to the road to avoid freezing to death, but the trackman refused. Mr. Henry had to walk to the First Section Fire Brigade to call and notify the Third Section to immediately send someone in a car to rescue him. However, too much time had passed, and he had been exposed to excessive cold. When the car arrived at Baolong Hospital, the doctor said that the injuries were not severe. Apart from some gasoline burns on his face, there were no injuries on his body. It was simply because he had been exposed to the cold for too long that he could not be saved. Now the coffin is still not closed, and it can be inspected. Please help us to expand the scope of assistance. Moreover, nearby residents said that after the accident, every time a fire truck passed by, they would hear screams for help. After the Third Section Fire Brigade's pumper truck set off, it was overtaken by Liu Rongtai's car on Baoshan Road. If rescue had been provided immediately after the train accident, Liu Rongtai would not have died. It is unreasonable that the firefighters did not notify the Third Section Fire Brigade when the fire truck passed by, as the truck had not yet passed at that time, and it would have been possible to call out. Moreover, the residents heard cries for help when the fire truck returned. If rescue had been provided in time, he would not have died. After a delay of three hours, even a healthy man would have frozen to death after lying in the wind and snow for three hours. Moreover, Liu Rongtai had already suffered shock. The personnel of the Railway Bureau sat idly by and did not provide rescue, neglecting their duties and disregarding human life, which is deeply hateful. You are all comrades of the Firefighting Federation. Please help us to provide assistance to extend our condolences and protect the lives of those who come after. After the report, all those present agreed that the Railway Bureau personnel had failed in their duties, resulting in Liu's tragic death. Moreover, Gonghe Xin Road is a key location, and three of the four gate leaves had been destroyed by armored vehicles. Two or three years had passed, and they had not been repaired. Before the repairs, more staff should have been assigned to hang red lights as a warning to avoid danger. The Railway Bureau had been slow to repair and did not hang red lights, which shows their incompetence. Liu left behind an elderly mother in her seventies, a young wife and concubine, and a ten-year-old son, a tragic sight. Is there anything more terrible than this? If we do not seriously negotiate, how can we comfort the spirit of the departed? It was decided that the Federation should seriously negotiate with the Railway Bureau to achieve its goals and petition the Municipal Government for generous compensation. Chen Weihan and Yao Xiangsheng were appointed to comfort Liu's family. The coffin will be closed immediately, and a funeral date will be chosen. Liu's funeral home will be set up at the Xiangshan Association on Qiujiang Road, and special representatives will be appointed to handle funeral affairs. The funeral expenses will be decided at a later date at a board meeting. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

New Construction of Zhabei Water and Electricity Plant 126

Yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, Committee Member Chu Minyi, accompanied by his wife and Zeng Guangming, the former Director of the Shandong Telegraph Bureau, visited the Zhang Huabang Zhabei Commercial Water and Electricity Plant. They were first accompanied by the plant's engineers, Pan Zhongyun, Shen Heting, and Li Rannan, to various parts of the power plant for detailed explanations. A view of the Water and Electricity Plant (photographed by Three Museums).

It was said that the plant had built a new plant and purchased two sets of water turbines from Czechoslovakia to be operated in rotation to prevent accidents. Since December 24 of the previous winter, supply had begun. The power plant can generate 10,000 open circuit watts per day, and the water plant can supply 12,000 English gallons. The most users use is 9,000 watts of electricity and 9,500 gallons of water. The exterior of the water plant building is entirely Eastern in style, with an engineer's residence and staff dormitory attached. The assets of the two plants are estimated at 11 million yuan. They all said goodbye and returned to Shanghai after 4 PM.

Further Correction to Dada Tobacco Factory's Accident 127

A letter from Dada Tobacco Factory states: "To the esteemed Editor of Shenbao, With respect, After reading Fuxin Tobacco Company's letter in yesterday's newspaper, which completely shirks responsibility, we were very surprised. We hereby present the details of the incident for the public's review. The day after the incident at our factory, we sent a letter to Fuxin Tobacco Company, stating that our factory was commissioned by your company to roll cigarettes, and all the spice mixing machines were borrowed from your company. Your company sent Mr. Zhu to manage the machines. At that time, Mr. Zhu neglected his duties and left his post without permission, resulting in the accident. It seems that our factory cannot bear the responsibility for this matter. After investigation, our factory suffered damage to the machines, and two male workers and twelve female workers were injured and sent to various hospitals for treatment. All future losses must be fully compensated by your company, etc. The mixing of spices for cigarette rolling is different for each factory. Fuxin Tobacco Company borrowed these machines because it did not want our factory to know its secrets, so it sent Mr. Zhu Guangbu and two old stewards to manage them themselves. Therefore, our factory has nothing to do with any responsibility, and the company should naturally bear the burden of the damage. All of the above are facts. Please publish this in your newspaper for correction. We will be very grateful. Respectfully, Dada Tobacco Factory. January 15, 20th year of the Republic of China."

Old Woman Dies After Broken Leg is Ultimately Unsaved 128

Determined to Have Been Hit and Killed by a Car

Lu Guishi, an old woman from Dachang, who was sixty-two years old this year, came to Shanghai a few days ago to visit her nephew's wife, Lu Zhang, at No. 81 Dakang Li, Kangti Road, in the French Concession. At 1 PM on the 14th, she went out and was hit by a No. 730 truck from the Engineering Department of the French Municipal Council, driven by driver Wang Zhiliang, while walking through the Caishi Road area. The old woman was unable to avoid it and was knocked down, injuring her left leg. The patrol police saw this, recorded the license plate number, and sent the injured person to Renji Hospital for treatment, and then reported back to the police chief for review. After Guishi was admitted to the hospital, the doctor found that her lower leg was severely injured and immediately amputated it in the hope of saving her life. However, it was still ineffective, and she died at 2 AM that night. The hospital notified the police station, who carried the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall for examination. Yesterday, the Traffic Department summoned Lu Zhang, a relative of the deceased, and the defendant to the case, and reported to Judge Zhu of the French Public Court, who inspected the scene and confirmed that the deceased had indeed been hit and killed by a car before her death. He ordered photographs to be taken and allowed the family to prepare a coffin for collection.

Opening a Gambling Den and Matching Handwriting 129

Xie Liansheng Has No Way to Deny

Fined and Sentenced to One Year Imprisonment

Xie Liansheng, a Ningbo native, was privately selling lamp black opium in a house at No. 1204 Hanbi Li Road. The day before yesterday afternoon, Western police chief Mr. Pan of the Traffic Department of the General Patrol Room secretly went with detectives and arrested Xie and opium smokers Tan Shaoqing, Shen Atian, Tang Longsheng, Lou Ada, Wang Qingji, and Tang Chunji, seizing opium paraphernalia and sutras. Yesterday, they were sent to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Xiao Xiefei proposed the case. Xie denied that the gambling den was set up by him, saying that he never smoked opium and would not open an opium den. None of the others admitted to being a seller of opium. Judge Xiao feared that someone would be wrongly released and ordered each defendant to write and compare handwriting with the seized sutras. Xie wrote "Pay 15 yuan," deliberately changing his handwriting. However, the written "yuan" character was mistakenly written with four strokes, and the "yuan" characters in the sutras were also all with four strokes. It was then determined that Xie was indeed the owner of the gambling den. At that time, Xie also lowered his head in silence. Therefore, he was sentenced to one year of imprisonment and a fine of 150 yuan. If he was unable to pay, he could commute two yuan to one day of imprisonment. Tang Chunji was found not guilty, and the others were sentenced to two months of imprisonment. The opium paraphernalia was confiscated.

He claimed he was mistakenly arrested while out shopping near Xiaomu Bridge. A man named Xie Xirong, 56 years old, from Taoyuan, worked at the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Plant, residing at No. 3, Wengjia Sand. A man named Liu Weiting, 55 years old, from Hunan, worked at the steel mill. There was also a local woman named Gu Mao Yin, 27 years old, who worked as a sock knitter, all residing next door at No. 3. Two other individuals, Zhou Changan, 27 years old, from Xuzhou, residing at Xin Xin Lane, Dapu Bridge, Jin Shenfu Road, in the French Concession, currently worked as a chef at the Xin Xin Jingchuan Restaurant; and Wang Deyou, 22 years old, from Anhui, residing at No. 2, Xing'an Lane, Guangdong Street, currently worked at a restaurant. Special News from the Shipping Industry 132

The Weisheng Steamship Collides and Damages Jardine Matheson's Weisheng Steamship. This time, coming from Guangdong to Shanghai, it encountered a severe storm with heavy snow. As the ship sailed near a lighthouse on the Shantou sea, it was late at night, and the wind and waves were particularly treacherous. The ship lost control, and its stern was hit by a huge wave near the lighthouse, striking against the reef. The stern hull was severely damaged. Fortunately, the engine was not damaged, so it was able to sail to Shanghai after the wind subsided. After arriving in Shanghai, it was immediately repaired and will be completed and ready to sail tomorrow. The cargo was not damaged, but the passengers were quite frightened.

Inland River Vessels Will Connect. The small inland river steamers connecting Jiangsu and Zhejiang have been blocked by ice. The routes to Suzhou, Huzhou, Changzhou, and Wuxi have been impassable for six days. Yesterday, the weather warmed up, and the section from Huangdu to Shanghai has thawed. There are still ice floes below Huangdu. The small steamers that were blocked, the Suzhou line, arrived yesterday and will resume regular service on Saturday. The Huzhou line originally planned to resume service yesterday morning, but because the route was not fully open, it was postponed for one day and will resume today. The Changzhou and Wuxi steamers should also arrive in Shanghai in the next two days.

Woolen Cloth Industry Requests Modification of New Tariff 133

The Highest Reaches 127% of Value

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Asks the Ministry of Finance to Find a Remedy

Fifty companies, including Jiufeng, Yida, Yikang, Chunhe Yong, Shixin, Huaxin, Fuchangxiang, Yukang, Xinchang, Shengchang, Huakang, Huasheng, Yuancheng, Yongchun, Heyong, Huashengxiang Yongfeng, Huafutai, Hengfeng, Qiafeng, Meilun, Dachangxiang, Rongchangxiang, and others, representatives of the woolen cloth industry in this city, believe that the newly established import tariff rates for woolen cloth are levied on a specific duty basis. Calculated as a percentage of price, the highest rate reaches 127% of the value, and even the lowest rate reaches 46%. This is a burden that woolen cloth merchants can hardly bear. After a meeting, they decided to send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting it to forward the request for modification to the Ministry of Finance. The original letter stated: "Upon investigation, the third category of the new tariff, 'wool and its products,' has a maximum duty rate of 40%, but this is limited to carpets and rugs, as they are luxury items and thus taxed the most heavily in this category, unlike other items. The request from these merchants pertains to specific duties under items 97A and 97B, and the ad valorem duties under item 97C should not exceed 30%. It is presumed that the survey of commodity prices at the time was inaccurate, resulting in a tax rate of 127% for the highest category and 46.5% for the lowest category. The other categories are all above 90% or 60%, which is the highest tax rate in any category of the new tariff. Not only is it difficult for woolen cloth merchants to bear, but it also does not comply with the maximum tax rate limit of the new tariff. The merchants' request for modification is very justified. However, the procedure for revising commodity prices is complicated and cannot be completed in a short period. If the excessive tax burden on these merchants is not resolved immediately, their business will be difficult to maintain. Could the Ministry, by analogy with item 90C, temporarily instruct the customs to levy taxes according to market prices? The fundamental revision of these two items should then be thoroughly investigated and coordinated by the commodity price office. This is currently the only way to resolve the difficulties of the industry." In addition to sending a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to forward their difficulties, representatives of the woolen cloth industry were also elected to visit the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, the Customs Administration, and the Jianghai Customs Office to personally deliver petitions.

Ministry of Industry Appoints Sugar Inspection Technical Officer 134

Deputy Director Cai of the Bureau of Standards, Metrology, and Inspection Concurrently Serves

Imported sugar products must undergo inspection. The former Ministry of Industry and Commerce promulgated regulations and ordered the Shanghai Bureau of Standards, Metrology, and Inspection to promptly plan for this. The Bureau believed that this inspection was a specialized undertaking that could not be handled without specialists. The Bureau's Chemical Inspection Department had only two senior technicians, and their workload was already heavy, making it difficult to handle additional tasks. Therefore, it was necessary to find specialists to take on the responsibility. Zhou Dayao, a Bachelor of Chemical Engineering from Purdue University in the United States and a Master of Sugar Engineering from Louisiana State University in the United States, and Wu Zhuo, a Bachelor of Chemical Engineering from the University of Ottawa in the United States and a Master of Sugar Engineering from Louisiana State University in the United States, both had profound knowledge and rich experience, having served as chemical technicians in British sugar factories. They are rare talents in China for sugar industry research. Therefore, the Ministry of Industry was requested to appoint them as technical officers for sugar product inspection at the Bureau to facilitate the work. In addition, in response to a previous telegram from the Ministry, Cai Wuji, the former Deputy Director of the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Institute of the former Ministry of Agriculture and Mining, was temporarily appointed as Deputy Director of the Bureau. Upon assuming his duties, it was found that the Bureau's Livestock and By-products Inspection Department urgently needed specialists. Deputy Director Cai graduated from the Grignon Agricultural School in France and the Alfort Veterinary School in France, obtaining degrees in agricultural technology and veterinary medicine. He has extensive knowledge and experience in veterinary medicine. Therefore, a request was made to appoint him concurrently as a technical officer in that department. Cai himself also expressed his agreement to use his expertise. The above three individuals have been approved and assigned to their respective positions.

A Laughing Matter 146

·Hai·Ke

A Shy Young Man (Visiting an old man) Old man, I've come to visit you. I actually have a very important matter and I need you to help me with.

Old Man You can tell me. If I can help, I won't refuse.

A Shy Young Man Yesterday your daughter came to see me. She... she told me that she loved me with all her heart...

Old Man So you came to see me today. Are you asking me to agree to you marrying her?

A Shy Young Man No. I'm only asking you to teach your daughter a lesson. She can't embarrass me like that again. I can't take it.

Judge (To a thief) You have repeatedly committed theft and have not reformed despite repeated warnings. I have no choice but to sentence you to three years in prison.

Thief Please, sir, be lenient and forgive me. Too many people are depending on me for food.

Judge Do you have many children?

Thief I don't have any children. But look at those who eat public meals. Aren't they indirectly depending on me for food? If I don't commit crimes, where will they get their food?

Woman Every time I look at the bright moon outside the window on a moonlit night, I always have inexplicable worries.

Man You might as well live in my attic room. There isn't even a window. I guarantee you won't have any worries.

The Story of the Qiao Sisters' Escape 147

Ms. Chen Baoqin

My old friend Mr. Wang is from Sichuan. He took ill last year and returned home from school. Now he has recovered and is coming east again. He arrived in Shanghai a few days ago. It is a great joy to meet an old friend again. Last night I gave him a welcome dinner. During the dinner, I asked about the recent situation in Sichuan. Mr. Wang lamented the lawless behavior of the warlords. He was especially saddened by a story of a warlord pursuing a woman. I wrote it down.

A certain warlord was based in Chengdu. He did not know the arts. However, due to his high position, if he was considered ignorant, it would be disrespectful. Therefore, he asked his secretary to prepare a draft, and after reading it, he lectured everywhere to gain people's trust. One day, he lectured at a girls' school. He saw two beautiful students sitting side by side. Although the warlord had dozens of concubines, he could not help but be captivated. The thought of seeking a phoenix suddenly arose. He returned and discussed it with his subordinates. It happened that one of his concubines was also enrolled in the girls' school, so he knew that the two girls were sisters, the daughters of a wealthy family named Yang in Chengdu. He also learned that Yang had a hibiscus addiction, so he sent someone to arrest him. He was fined more than 100,000 taels of gold. The Yang family was caught in this dramatic change and had no way out. The two girls suddenly remembered that the warlord had a concubine who was their classmate, so they went to ask for help. The concubine was very enthusiastic in order to gain favor. However, she could not do anything herself, but she was willing to introduce the two girls to the warlord. The two girls were eager to save their father. Therefore, they went to see him in shame. The warlord pretended not to know and asked the two girls why they had come. The two girls told him everything. The warlord pretended to be angry and asked who had done it. He insisted on finding him. He ordered Yang's father to be released quickly and apologized to the two girls. He also treated them with great courtesy. He kept them for dinner and then sent them back. Yang's father, under this lascivious power, although he knew the tricks, did not dare not cooperate. After returning home, he set up a grand banquet to thank him for his kindness. The wine was delicious and the music was wonderful. The secretary asked to arrange a marriage. Yang's father pretended to agree. But please wait a few days to buy all the dowry. The warlord

Legal Anecdotes 148

·Bi·Ren

The Republic of Estonia is a small country along the Baltic Sea. Recently, a difficult legal issue arose. It has become an interesting story. According to the law of the country, anyone convicted of a capital crime has the right to choose their method of execution. There are two methods: taking poison or hanging. Recently, a prisoner sentenced to death volunteered to take poison. The executioner gave him the poison. The prisoner publicly swallowed it without fear. However, after taking the poison, he did not die. He only suffered from illness for a few weeks and then fully recovered. He became even more resistant to this type of poison. This made the country's authorities very embarrassed. According to the law, the amount of poison given to the prisoner is strictly regulated. It cannot be exceeded. If he is given it repeatedly, it is inhumane. The prisoner refused to be hanged. It is his right. Therefore, it is difficult to handle. It is likely that the prisoner will not die and will regain his freedom. In terms of law, the punishment he has received has been executed once.

The warlord knew that he had been fooled. He conducted a large-scale search. The Yang family had disappeared. Although the warlord was furious, there was nothing he could do. After the Liu family arrived in Yixing, they sent a letter to the warlord and scolded him bitterly. It was a happy thing.

Anecdotes About the Four-Gilled Perch 149

Qingsong Jushi

Mr. Zhang Shileng (Zhang Xianghe) of my hometown, after becoming famous, held various official positions both inside and outside the country. He seemed to have forgotten the local flavor. After retiring and returning to his hometown, it happened to be the autumn and winter season. He imitated Zhang Jiying's desire to eat perch sashimi. He ordered the cook to buy it and cook it. The cook was from Jiangsu and did not know the method. He did not wash off the thin membrane on the skin and cooked it in the pot. After Mr. Zhang tasted it, he felt the flavor was ordinary and greasy. He said that he had not tasted the local flavor of his hometown for decades. Now that he finally had it, it was not as good as before. Could it be that the thing has changed? How confused was the old gentleman of poetry and wine! Zuo Wenxiang Gong Zongtang opened the government in Liangjiang and came to Songjiang for a great review. He heard that the four-gilled perch of Songjiang had a unique taste. He ordered his military officer to buy it and eat it. For a time, it was difficult to find. He bought the flower drum fish, commonly known as the carp fish, which was similar in shape but had no gills on its head and scales on its body. He gave it as a gift. The Gong did not know. When eating, his lips and cheeks salivated. He savored it with relish. After returning to the governor's office, he still talked about it happily with his colleagues, saying that it was a happy event in his life. How easy it is to deceive a gentleman!

Feng Haosou (Feng Menglao) of Jintan retired and lived in Shanghai. He learned when the delicious food of my hometown would be on the market. He took a car to Songjiang and bought more than a dozen perch to take away. He was overjoyed. But the cook he hired did not cook it properly. He fried it with soy sauce, wine, and vinegar instead of cooking it with pickled meat soup. Haosou ate it. It was greasy and tasteless, and the sour smell touched his nose. He said that the delicious food was not delicious. Why does the product of Songjiang have a false reputation? Alas, he blamed the product instead of the cook. Haosou's original name was true to his name. He failed this delicious food.

A Short Note on Reading Paintings on a Snowy Day 150

Ke Ding'an

On the ninth day of the first month of the twentieth year, the jade shavings were flying and the north wind was howling. The Shanghai China Art College opened its second exhibition of calligraphy and paintings at the Ningbo Fellow Association. I have a deep love for it. I went to see it despite the wind and snow to broaden my horizons. When I arrived, there were already more than a hundred people before me. Surrounded by them, I felt like I was in the city of the Jade Capital. The ten colors and five lights were dazzling. In addition to the works of teachers and students of the school, there were also many calligraphy and paintings by famous people. Such as Ma Xiangbo, Cai Yuanpei, Huang Ainong, Zheng Sucan, Wu Daiqiu, Yan Ganyuan, and Li Zuhang. Mr. Han and other gentlemen all have excellent works to participate in. I felt even more precious. The products of the teachers and students of the school amounted to more than 500 pieces. Ma Mengrong's wisteria and myna was titled. The wonderful sound breaks the moon, and the purple ribbon is colorful without the dawn wind. Mengrong's wisteria was previously appreciated by Watanabe Chenmu of Japan. This work is more refined than before. A frame of ink crabs imitates the style of the Yuan Dynasty. The brushstrokes are elegant and outstanding, just like his people. Other works, such as Qiuyuan Yiqu, are light and elegant, and full of poetic meaning. Several frames of autumn chrysanthemums also have their advantages. Mengrong once said that painting is valuable because of its natural interest. If you only copy, you will be a craftsman. This is true. Zhang Shanzhen has a frame of fierce tiger, titled. According to the strict downward view, take advantage of the situation and wait for the time. A humble gentleman, danger is like peace. Lifelike and real, it is a masterpiece. Zhang Daqian's crabapple was titled. Falling leaves rang Xing Lang, the west wind blows old goose side frost. No one leans on the stone fence in the middle of the night, leaving the remaining fireflies to illuminate the crabapple. There is also a frame of hibiscus, titled. The autumn water is clear, and the hibiscus is beautiful when it comes out of the water. She wants to pick it when she crosses the river. No, that beauty is far away. Other landscapes and other works are free and unique. It is a rare hand in modern times. Zhang Guangzhi's long scroll of hundreds of flowers is exquisitely detailed. Women can get this, which makes men ashamed. There are so many masterpieces that I can't describe them one by one. When I write this late at night, the scene at that time is still jumping in my mind.

Record of Deng Fen Weng's Book Carving Exhibition 151

Du Juan

Deng Zi Fen Weng. I did not know him initially, but vaguely heard that he was as clear as fire and snow. Weng had been studying the arts since childhood, especially devoting himself to epigraphy and calligraphy. He was blessed with genius and complemented it with scholarly effort, deepening his attainments. However, Weng had an eccentric personality and did not conform to the world. He liked to use wine to dispel his feelings and also enjoyed traveling. He indulged in Chan Buddhist pleasure. Many famous mountains and forests in Jiangsu and Zhejiang bear his ink traces. I remember his five-character律詩 (lǜshī, a type of regulated verse) when I traveled to Hupao Temple years ago, saying: "Understanding Zhao Zhou's interest, hearing the ancient bell in the mountains. A lamp coldly faces the rain, a thousand gāthās (Buddhist verses) arise from sitting in the wind. The bone-piercing fragrance is exquisite, seeking the source of flowing water. There is no great medicine for longevity, the fragrant meaning fills the boundless." One can imagine his person from this. Weng recently exhibited his personal calligraphy and carvings at Jue Lin. I went to see it yesterday and saw the walls covered in splendid, clear scrolls. The six-foot stone drum screen does not use the meaning of Chang Shuo, but slightly imitates Zhao Yi Shu, possessing a distinct style. The seal script obtains Li Si's method, full of ancient charm. A small vertical axis in regular script, less than two feet, writes Li Bai's poem, revealing its ingenuity. The large couplets in official script have a powerful and vigorous spirit, directly seizing the seat of Yi Tingzhou. His cursive script has the momentum of a phoenix soaring and a dragon flying, seemingly from the method of Suo Shao Bao. I chose a four-foot couplet and will buy it to take home. The horizontal scrolls presented, made in large and small seal scripts, are especially outstanding. Weng is especially proficient in epigraphy. A hundred volumes of his printed catalogs were displayed in the hall, divided into two volumes, upper and lower, with vermilion seals on plain paper, dazzlingly brilliant. This is due to his deep understanding of the Qin and Han dynasties, and his vigorous wrist strength, creating a unique style.

Parisian Tales 152

(5) 6 Once Lived in Paris

Inside the cell of a condemned man, Tony Ska saw the ragged, feverish, trembling prisoner, who had no strength left to support himself before his execution. Tony Ska was deeply moved with compassion. She first tried to move him emotionally, and then gave him much encouragement. While the fierce executioner was waiting in the next room for the time to come to carry out the execution, Tony Ska made the condemned man play with the toys the small merchant had given her, making him as happy as a child. At dawn, the condemned man went to be executed. But he retained a most beautiful memory in his mind. The film reached this point, and I personally felt it should be silent. But the producers inserted a prayerful song here. I think this is the only flaw in the film. Sound films often have this defect.

When Tony Ska returned to the brothel, her sisters and the brothel's customers ridiculed her, calling her the "hangman's widow." Afterwards, everyone avoided her as an ominous object. Soon she was driven out of the brothel and had to wander the streets. Her nickname "hangman's widow" remained. She was often bullied on the streets.

One night she met her fiancé. Her fiancé took her back to the village to prepare for the wedding. The night before the wedding, her fiancé met friends who often gathered at a hotel. A small merchant told him, "I also know a woman named Tony Ska. This woman is very beautiful. Everyone calls her the 'hangman's widow.'" Then he told the story and produced Tony Ska's photo as proof. Tony Ska's fiancé, hearing this, immediately ran to denounce her severely. She fled from the insults of the entire village.

Warmth in the Heart 153

(350) Bao Tian Xiao

Seventeenth: Returning for Lasting Beauty, Rouge and Kohl Muddying the Eyebrows; Seeking Life Extension, a Golden Market for Swift Horses.

Let us say that Zuo Shi Chen hosted a party at Lü Yi's place. A female great person, Ren Pei Zhen, came to the banquet. Those present were also very welcoming to her. This welcome, in fact, was entirely out of curiosity. Everyone thought in their hearts that this female great person must be awe-inspiring and outstanding. They all wanted to see her to broaden their horizons. But when they saw her, they felt that she was no different from an ordinary lady. In conversation, she was very modest and did not adopt an intimidating posture. She was also very polite to the people in their room, not putting on airs at all. As they spoke about the previous organization of the women's revolutionary army, Ren Pei Zhen said, "Carrying that gun while walking really felt cumbersome. At first, I thought the weight of a gun was limited, only ten or twenty jin (a Chinese unit of weight) or so. But I realized that the more you carry it, the heavier it gets. The saying 'no light burden beyond a hundred steps' is true. I was fine because I naturally had unbound feet. But two of my sisters, their feet were 'enlarged feet,' swaying from side to side, how could they walk? After not even two li (a Chinese unit of distance), their faces were already flushed and they were short of breath. Later, we couldn't bear it, saying that not being able to walk was unavoidable, but their determination to join the army, this ambition, was truly admirable." Zuo Shi Chen said, "It was because at that time, regardless of men or women, everyone was of one mind, that the revolution succeeded in overthrowing the Manchu government. Actually, women don't necessarily have to join the army. There are many things that can be done in the rear, such as nursing wounded soldiers, measuring the clothes needed by soldiers. It's the same as contributing to the country. Why must they carry guns to the front? Even if they want guns, wouldn't it be much better to get a few lighter pistols?" Ren Pei Zhen laughed, "You really speak of peace too easily. At that time, it was already not easy to get a gun. How could you choose to pick the best pistols? A few pistols were not even enough for the officers to carry, how could they be popularized to so many people? Even for our women's revolutionary army, getting twenty guns was already very troublesome. They said, 'Your guns are just for show. Anyway, you may not go to the front line to fire, so it doesn't matter if they are subpar.' Just think about this sentence, wouldn't it infuriate people? It clearly scolds our women's revolutionary army, saying that anyway, they are just for show." Zuo Shi Chen said, "It's not quite like that. Physiologically speaking, the constitution of women is very different from that of men. In any country, women have no obligation to serve in the military. However, in revolutionary times, women were already citizens and of course aroused a sense of righteousness. In our history, there have been female generals, but few female soldiers. Because managing the camp may require knowledgeable and outstanding talents, but ultimately, charging into battle is not a woman's business." Ren Pei Zhen nodded and said, "So in the end, it was disbanded. Honestly, everyone also complained about enduring this hardship."

Being Continuously Affected by Foreign Exchange Changes, Foreign Exchange Foreign Merchant Banks Suffered the Most Damage. This Time the Lunar New Year Has Just Passed, and the Customary Qingli Lunar New Year Is Approaching in the Blink of an Eye. General Commerce Has No Special Opportunity to Develop, and It Is Quite Difficult to Wind Up. According to people in the financial industry, the current time to end the books is only one month away. Most of the overdue items have not been initiated. Banks that do foreign exchange or operate on behalf of customers are mostly at a loss. According to the past results of the money shop's collection of outstanding funds, the recovery rate is not even 10-20%. If it is in this port, we can try our best to find ways to promote the industry, but in foreign ports, it is often beyond our reach, and it is difficult to repay on time. Therefore, at present, in the money industry, engaging in collection procedures is exceptionally busy. The bank's own money supply has gradually become abundant, but there is no place to settle it. Therefore, the money supply is now gradually falling again.

Distant Futures of Cotton Yarn Industry: External Observers' Perspective 160

The yarn market remains firm, with actual sales still sluggish. Dealers from various regions maintain a neutral attitude. However, a shipment to Chongqing, Sichuan, bought 3-400 bales. There are no other signs of excitement. Therefore, people's sentiments are still stable. However, the situation is quite tight, as the bulls' pulling power is very strong and shows no sign of loosening. Recently, one manufacturer has settled, which has eased the market atmosphere. External observers are consistently bullish about the distant futures. The future prospects will depend on actual sales.

The Marked-Price Standard is Stable and Correct. At the opening of the marked-price market, the buying interest was very strong, with near-term prices rising 5-6 qian, and distant prices rising 3-4 qian. The second session was slightly weaker, falling 1-2 qian. The market closed strong again, resulting in price changes of 2, 3, and 6 qian across different months. In the afternoon, due to the return of adulterated Three-Grade Yarn and the continued rise in gold prices, the market atmosphere rose again, resulting in near-term prices falling 6 qian and distant prices rising 1, 2, and 5 qian. The total transaction volume for the day was 45,850 bales. The sales records showed that Yongchang sold 2,000 bales, Rongxing 1,700 bales, Hengde 1,700 bales, Yixu 1,000 bales, Hengchang 1,150 bales, and the rest sold 6, 7, and 800 bales each. The purchases records showed that Changfeng bought 1,900 bales, Guangdong 1,600 bales, Dafeng 900 bales, and the rest bought 5, 6, 7, and 800 bales each. The closing prices are recorded as follows:

Bullish Sentiment is Strong in the Cotton Market 161

The cotton market remains firm. The overseas cotton market is mediocre. However, gold prices are trending higher, and exchange rates are shrinking significantly, leading to high silver prices for foreign cotton. Therefore, the bullish sentiment is strong, and the pulling power is becoming tighter. Although spot cotton business is slow, those holding goods are very keen on hoarding, so the situation feels particularly tight. However, Hengde and Gongtai settled 2-30,000 dan of American cotton.

Grain: River-Transported Rice Market in Shanghai Turns Downward 163

Zhabei: Yesterday, the total number of sources arriving from various regions was around 20. Buying interest in the local market has become sluggish. Northern japonica rice has fallen back by 2 jiao, but special japonica rice is still around 14 yuan. Ordinary transactions are dull and the market is stagnant. The overall trend is quite soft. Thin early rice, upon inspection, seemed level, showing a slight jiao. Foreign indica rice sales are still acceptable, with sources arriving successively, and prices dropping nearly 1 chi. The markets for Du-tipped and Bu-tipped rice are uninspired, but as goods are scarce, the market is stable. Bian-Yuan and Diao-Wei rice shops are not deserted, and prices are uniquely stable. Yin-Yuan rice is stagnant and spiritless, but the owners are unwilling to sell at lower prices. The overall situation is one of flatness.

South Shanghai: Yesterday, there were not many sources arriving from the river. Market sales were mediocre. Changshu, Wuxi, Suzhou, and Tongzhou japonica rice have mostly been stagnant and fatigued by half a jiao. This is truly because of sluggish sales in both urban and rural areas. Although there is a small demand for early thin rice from the Southern regions, there are still bottom goods. After dark, the number of shipments gradually increased, and the market went from stable to fatigued. Yang Du and various tipped rice varieties also felt a shift towards laxity. There were few transactions between the two sides. The market top barely opened at 12 yuan and 2 jiao, which was level with the previous day. The arrival and sales of Bian Yin-Yuan rice were both sluggish, with no changes for the time being.

Jiangxi Late Rice Sales are Active and Continue to Rise 164

Ningxiang Indica Rice Alone Trends Weak.

Yesterday's market conditions for out-of-town indica rice: Jiangxi and Nanjing routes both continued to arrive, but the number of arrivals was not large, and they were scattered small orders. Jiangxi rice was being sought after in the local market. Yesterday, Guangdong merchants continued to try to buy, with prices for high and low grades all rising nearly one jiao. Over 3,000 bags of late-harvest machine-milled rice were offered throughout the market, with prices ranging from 11 yuan and 7 jiao to 11 yuan. Although Nanjing rice continued to arrive, local customers did not welcome it. Yesterday, the local market accommodated only 250 bags, with the price initially opening at 10 yuan, then falling to 9 yuan and 9 jiao. Mid-grade goods still need to be discounted. It will be difficult to open high-grade goods above 10 yuan in the future. Market prices are about 1 jiao lower than the previous day.

Flour and Wheat Market Initially Lively, Then Flat 165

Widespread Rumors That Factories Will Continue to Order 20,000 Tons of Australian Wheat

Wheat: Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed a pattern of being lively initially, then flat in the afternoon. In the morning, with positive reports about foreign wheat and continued increases in the gold market, the atmosphere in the market for each month was quite tense, about 3-4 fen better than the previous day's closing price. Until the opening of the afternoon session, with the flour market slightly soft and the previously rumored continuation of orders for Australian wheat by factories at over 20,000 tons, selling became smoother, and the market fell back. Looking at the situation in the future, if there are any further changes abroad, the market situation will inevitably change. As a result, the current month was 1 fen better than the previous day, February was down 1 fen, March was down 1 fen, April was unchanged, May was down 1 fen, and June's new wheat had not traded smoothly, with prices slightly less than expected.

Flour: Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market atmosphere for each month improved by 1-2 jiao due to better prices for foreign wheat, and benchmark gold prices soared again. People inside and outside the industry could not help but turn, and the market prices for each month rose about 1 fen compared to the previous day's closing price. Until the opening of the afternoon session, with gold prices slightly softer, people's sentiments softened again, and although there were few sellers on the market, the market loosened again. As a result, there was no change in January and February, March was up 2.5 li, April was up 5 li, May was up 7.5 li, and June was up 5 li.

Standard Futures Soybeans Rise Nearly 1 Qian 166

Soybean Cake Futures Also Rise Accordingly

Soybeans: Yesterday, the soybean market was firm due to the tight and rising reports from Dalian the previous day and a small number of short coverings in the morning. Each term rose by as much as 0.5 to 1 qian. The March term reached 4 taels and 6 qian, and people's sentiments were very good. After the opening of the afternoon session, out-of-town merchants suddenly sold off, but fortunately, the buying interest was still not weak, and benchmark gold prices fluctuated, so it only flattened slightly. As a result, it was 4 fen higher than the previous day for the January term, 6 fen higher for the February term, 7 fen higher for the March term, 9 fen higher for the April term, and 8 fen higher for the May term.

Soybean Cake: Yesterday, the cake market opened exceptionally well, with strong buying interest from all sides. The board uniformly rose by about 2 fen. Until the opening of the afternoon session, due to the weakening of the soybean situation and the slightly selling by oil factories and the selling by Dalian merchants, it turned slightly lower by nearly 1 fen. As a result, March was up 1.25 fen, April was up 2 fen, May was up 2.25 fen, and June was up 1.5 fen.

North-South Goods: Xiamen Sun-Dried Meat Rises 20 Taels 167

Xiamen Sun-Dried Pork: Recently, due to a long-term lack of supply and thin reserves, and with the prices of miscellaneous goods rising frequently, the situation is very tight. Seafood: Guang Belly Sells at Steadily Rising Prices 168

Top-Grade Shark Fins are Out of Stock

The Guang belly that previously arrived had already been sold out. It was not until recently that a small number arrived, but it coincided with a strong buying interest from various regions, resulting in insufficient supply. The market rose again and again. Yesterday, the offered prices were 308 taels for three boxes of top-grade belly, 286 taels for one box of large-face belly, and 257.5 taels for three boxes of two-face belly, which is a huge increase of 6-70 taels per grade compared to last year. And the merchants, regardless of the high prices, still want to buy, and the tightness of the market can be described as unparalleled.

Top-grade shark fins such as dragon beard and phoenix tail are all out of stock. There is also not much in the lower-middle grade street stocks. Merchants are peddling Jinshan top-grade fins for 480 taels, large-grade fins for 400 taels, 360-370 taels, medium-grade fins for 320 taels, and small-grade fins for 230-240 taels. Merchants from Hunan and Hubei have made purchases.

Silk, Tea, Foreign Firms: Silk Market is Quiet and Firm 169

Yesterday, telegrams from European and American factory agents continued to arrive in Shanghai. Due to limited raw materials and high costs, the factory side is adopting a wait-and-see attitude. Yesterday, only Taihe, etc., imported 50 bales of white factory silk to Shanghai, and Suichang imported 40 bales of yellow factory silk to Sichuan, all at firmly rising prices.

Wuxi Silk Factories: 40 Have Already Resumed Operations 170

The Wuxi silk factory industry was sluggish in silk sales last winter, and all silk factories traditionally took a holiday at the end of the year. Since the beginning of the year, the sales of European and American factory agents have been very strong, and silk prices have soared. In addition, the government silk factory bond issuance is imminent, so various silk factories have resumed operations separately after the 5th. Among the 50+ silk factories in the county, 40 have already resumed operations, and the rest will also find ways to resume operations within the next few days.

High-Grade Gunpowder Green Tea and Pearl Tea Sales are Smooth in France 171

Yesterday, foreign firms in the local tea market, the Zhenmei aged teas from Tunxi, Suian, and other routes, as well as Qiahe, Tongfu, Yongxing and other firms, were still making every effort to search and buy due to low tea prices. The total transaction volume throughout the city was over 1,400 boxes, and the selling prices remained unchanged. Huang Xiyi, Bai and Zhuang Fulin Foreign Firm, also had many [transactions]. Prices opened at 21-22 [yuan]. The current inventory in the market is only over 30,000 boxes, and people's sentiments are stable. However, various European firms are still determined not to [buy] unless the price is low, and it is difficult to expect tea prices to return to high levels.

Piece Goods and Woolens: Market Prices Change Three Times a Day 172

Since the implementation of the new tariff, the prices of woolens have been rising steadily. All light goods such as beiges, genuine tribute flannel, Walter cloth, and all woolen fabrics must be calculated according to weight. Those weighing no more than 6 English ounces per square [yard] must be taxed 280 gold yuan per dan. Those weighing between 6 and 12 English ounces [yard] are taxed 250 gold yuan, which is 2-3 times higher than the old tax. Therefore, the industry has decided to temporarily raise prices by about 30%, but they still feel that the price is too expensive and the volume of sales is low, resulting in a distinction between official and unofficial prices. However, those who need it urgently will sell at temporary price increases. It can truly be said that morning and evening prices are different, with the idea that prices change three times a day. Therefore, the recent selling prices of woolens have no standards, and the speed of change is the same as the wild ups and downs of the benchmark gold market.

Coal: Fushun Coal Dust Spot Goods Sold Out 173

Fushun coal dust, a major fuel for factories, has recently seen a sharp decline in imports, resulting in a severe shortage of spot goods and soaring prices. Although various factories and coal dealers have tried their best to search for it, as of yesterday, there were no spot goods sold on the market. There are occasional futures transactions, but they are mostly for selling short. [Foreign] firm orders have generally not been sold recently, and no new goods have been shipped. Yesterday's market offer price had reached 12 taels and 5 qian per ton.

Oil Market: Asphalt Nearing Close 174

The asphalt market has been unstable in recent months. Due to a poor harvest the previous year, the reserves on the Han River in the late autumn were very thin, with only 2-3,000 pieces stored throughout the market. However, Shanghai merchants had more reserves than the Han market, reaching 8-9,000 pieces, preparing for the autumn oil extraction. However, soap factories did not process it, and oil extraction was also slow. By the winter, new goods had appeared in the production area, and Shanghai merchants still had 5-6,000 pieces in stock. As a result, they became wary and had to sell at lower prices. The price of Chong Jing asphalt fell from 22 taels to 20 taels, but the price on the Han market was still 18 taels. The decline in Shanghai's price can be said to be meaningless. Therefore, after the new goods entered the market, merchants, due to unsold inventory, all stood by and watched. However, the arrival of oil from Taizhou, Zhejiang, forced the opening of the market. The initial opening price was around 19 taels. To date, more than 1,000 dan have arrived. The recent price has opened at 18 taels due to a slight decline in the Han market, but because the quality of Taizhou oil varies, the price cannot be considered standard. According to yesterday's telegram from the Han market, the price of front-row Macheng oil has fallen to 14 taels and 8 qian, and the price of back-row goods is 14 taels and 6 qian, but considering that it was still 18 taels half a month ago, it has also fallen sharply. And the price of branded Chong Jing, according to the previous letter from the Han market, has also fallen to 16 taels [per dan]. After this decline, the market may stabilize, and the price decline in the local market should be able to stabilize. However, it is said that the sales of Youxi, Neiping, Benche, and other oils from Zhejiang have been high since their release, so they may not depreciate with the Han market. However, the sales volume of candle [and tallow] in the winter was far less than in previous years. Although the reserves are thin, how can we clear sales? We must also worry about that.

Correspondence on Medical Consultations 175

Yang Yanhe

To Mr. Fu Zongyi: Your illness belongs to the category of flaccidity. The "Ling Shu Jing Mai Pian" (Classic of Spiritual Pivot, Meridians) says, "Deficiency causes flaccidity, unable to sit and rise." However, your letter is brief, and details regarding your appetite, bowel movements, presence of pain, accompanying symptoms, and age are not mentioned. Thus, a diagnosis is impossible. Upon examination, flaccidity has various types: tendon flaccidity, summer flaccidity, pulse flaccidity, heat flaccidity, muscle flaccidity, spleen deficiency flaccidity, spleen excess flaccidity, skin and hair flaccidity, bone flaccidity, damp-heat flaccidity, damp fatigue flaccidity, qi deficiency flaccidity, yin deficiency flaccidity, blood deficiency flaccidity, blood stasis flaccidity, qi deficiency with fatigue flaccidity, qi and blood deficiency flaccidity, kidney and liver deficiency flaccidity, food stagnation flaccidity, and so on. It cannot be determined arbitrarily. There is a single prescription that you may try. Take two chestnuts that are flat on both sides; those flat on one side and round on the other are useless. Place them at the head of your bed before going to sleep. Before dawn, before speaking, first take one, chew it in bed with your lips closed, chew it until it melts like a paste, and swallow it in three gulps, mentally guiding it to the dantian (lower abdomen). Then, take another one and chew and swallow it as before. After eating, sleep soundly. Do this every day. After half a month, if it is effective, you can stop taking the medicine. Recovery may occur within a hundred days.

To Mr. Huan Tang: Unsatisfactory coughing and phlegm: dry phlegm belongs to the lungs, salty taste belongs to the kidneys, and substantial texture belongs to the spleen. Speculating from this, the lungs, spleen, and kidneys are all diseased. However, your letter does not clearly state your body type (fat or thin), age, changes in appetite, bowel regularity, sleep quality, or any accompanying symptoms. Moreover, coughing as a disease has various types: heart cough, liver cough, spleen cough, lung cough, kidney cough, stomach cough, gallbladder cough, large intestine cough, small intestine cough, bladder cough, triple burner cough, pericardium cough, dry cough, hot cough, morning cough, sleep cough, before noon cough, afternoon cough, five-watch cough (early morning), less cough in the day and more at night, and so on. It cannot be treated carelessly. However, for a long-term cough, a single prescription involves using aged jellyfish skin, thoroughly rinsed, mixed with rock sugar, steamed, and eaten. Another prescription involves one pig lung, two qian (approx. 7.5 grams) of Sichuan yuan powder, three qian of baked ginger, and two fen (approx. 0.75 grams) of ephedra. Simmer it lightly in clear water and eat it. Eating it several times consecutively is effective.

To Mr. Dai Zhongfan: The fundamental treatment for this dizziness should be to tonify the liver and kidneys, which is essentially the same as the Western method of nourishing the brain, and may even be more effective. Your brain nerves were injured from a fall at the age of three. Nourishing the kidneys will nourish the brain because the brain is connected to the spinal cord within the kidneys. Its origin lies in the deficiency of the liver body and excess of liver function, causing upward rebellion towards the stomach. It must be that dizziness and vomiting occur upon rising, and the vomiting subsides and the dizziness reduces when lying down. Each episode requires several days of quiet sleep to recover. If the symptoms are as described, then the Liu Wei Di Huang Wan (Six Flavor Rehmannia Pill) should be the main treatment, with adjustments. If your body type is fat and fair, it is appropriate to combine clearing fire, resolving phlegm, and tonifying qi. If your body type is dark and thin, it is appropriate to combine nourishing yin, reducing fire, and calming the liver. As for the folk remedy, find glutinous rice flour from seven different families, (except those with the same surname), from each province, and save it for the Qingming Festival. In advance, pick tender willow shoots (the light yellow buds growing in the willow branches), one for each year of age, totaling twelve. Use the aforementioned rice flour to wrap small yuanxiao (glutinous rice balls), using the willow shoots as filling. Have him sit on the doorstep, facing inside the house, and eat them on the morning of Qingming Festival. Perhaps this can eliminate the root of the problem.

To Mr. Wang Weifeng: I am not skilled in surgery and cannot offer assistance. Please consult with Dr. Zhang Zanchen at 503 Xiyangguan Lane, Xizang Road. Dr. Zhang not only has a family tradition in internal and external medicine but also cares deeply for his patients. I hereby introduce you to him.

(Note) For those seeking medical advice, please send letters directly to Dr. Yang's clinic at No. 80 Anshun Lane, Kangti Road. I will reply with a special letter. This publication will not receive letters on my behalf.

Guidelines for Social News Submissions

(1) Text should be related to domestic and foreign science, industry, commerce, agriculture, (2) public health, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life, etc. Illustrations are limited to lyrical paintings related to various aspects of social life.

(3) Photographs that qualify include those of seasonal events, landscapes, flora and fauna, people, and news-related images. Photographs of scenic spots and scenery featuring fashionable women are especially welcome.

(4) The length of each text article should not exceed two thousand words.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(6) Do not write the manuscript horizontally, and do not write illegibly. Minimize the use of Western text; if it is absolutely necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink for drawings, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(8) Please indicate "Social News Editorial Department Received" on submissions.

(9) Submissions will not be returned, regardless of whether they are published or not. If a return is required, it must be stated in advance, and sufficient postage must be attached.

(10) Remuneration for text is divided into three categories: three yuan, two yuan, and one yuan per thousand words. The same applies to drawings and photographs per piece. Special submissions will be compensated separately.

Guidelines for Youth Corner Submissions 177

(1) Text should be within the scope of discussions on youth issues, domestic and foreign studies, or student news, essays, depictions of school life, and personal reflections. The style is not restricted.

(2) Illustrations are limited to those related to youth issues.

(3) Qualified photographs include those of youth life (such as sports, travel, excursions, plays, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements. Both individuals and groups are welcome. (4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) The length of each text article should not exceed two thousand words.

(6) Do not write the manuscript horizontally, and do not write illegibly. Minimize the use of Western text; if it is absolutely necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink for drawings, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(8) Please indicate "Youth Corner Editorial Department Received" on submissions.

(9) Submissions will not be returned, regardless of whether they are published or not. If a return is required, it must be stated in advance.

(10) Remuneration for text is divided into three categories: three yuan, two yuan, and one yuan per thousand words. The same applies to drawings and photographs per piece. Special submissions will be compensated separately.
